        function EquipWeapon(p9)
            if p9 then
                if plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(p9) then
                    plr.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(p9))
                end
            end
        end
        function weaponSc(p10)
            local v11, v12, v13 = pairs(plr.Backpack:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v14

                v13, v14 = v11(v12, v13)

                if v13 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v14:IsA('Tool') and v14.ToolTip == p10 then
                    EquipWeapon(v14.Name)
                end
            end
        end

        function vu19.Alive(p20)

        function vu19.Pos(_, p22)
            return (Root.Position - mode.Position).Magnitude <= p22
        end
        function vu19.Dist(p23, p24)
            return (Root.Position - p23:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart').Position).Magnitude <= p24
        end
        function vu19.DistH(p25, p26)
            return p26 < (Root.Position - p25:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart').Position).Magnitude
        end
        function vu19.Kill(p27, p28)
            if p27 and p28 then
                if not p27:GetAttribute('Locked') then
                    p27:SetAttribute('Locked', p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
                end

                PosMon = p27:GetAttribute('Locked').Position

                BringEnemy()
                EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)

                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool').ToolTip ~= 'Blox Fruit' then
                    _tp(p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(180), 0))
                else
                    _tp(p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0))
                end
                if RandomCFrame then
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(25, 30, 0))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25))
                    wait(0.5)
                    _tp(p27.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0))
                end
            end
        end

        function vu19.Mas(p35, p36)
            if p35 and p36 then
                if not p35:GetAttribute('Locked') then
                    p35:SetAttribute('Locked', p35.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame)
                end

                PosMon = p35:GetAttribute('Locked').Position

                BringEnemy()

                if p35.Humanoid.Health > HealthM then
                    weaponSc('Melee')
                    _tp(p35.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0))
                else
                    _tp(p35.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0))
                    Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'Z')
                    Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'X')
                    Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'C')
                    Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'V')
                    Useskills('Blox Fruit', 'F')
                end
            end
        end

        function statsSetings(p39, p40)
            if p39 == 'Melee' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Melee', p40)
                end
            elseif p39 == 'Defense' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Defense', p40)
                end
            elseif p39 == 'Sword' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Sword', p40)
                end
            elseif p39 == 'Gun' then
                if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                    replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Gun', p40)
                end
            elseif p39 == 'Devil' and plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
                replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('AddPoint', 'Demon Fruit', p40)
            end
        end
        function BringEnemy()
            if _B then
                local v41, v42, v43 = pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

                while true do
                    local v44

                    v43, v44 = v41(v42, v43)

                    if v43 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if v44:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and (v44.Humanoid.Health > 0 and (v44.PrimaryPart.Position - PosMon).Magnitude <= 250) then
                        v44.PrimaryPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(PosMon)
                        v44.PrimaryPart.CanCollide = true
                        v44:FindFirstChild('Humanoid').WalkSpeed = 0
                        v44:FindFirstChild('Humanoid').JumpPower = 0

                        if v44.Humanoid:FindFirstChild('Animator') then
                            v44.Humanoid.Animator:Destroy()
                        end

                        plr.SimulationRadius = math.huge
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        function Useskills(p45, p46)
            if p45 == 'Melee' then
                weaponSc('Melee')

                if p46 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p46 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                elseif p46 == 'C' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'C', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'C', false, game)
                end
            elseif p45 == 'Sword' then
                weaponSc('Sword')

                if p46 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p46 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                end
            elseif p45 == 'Blox Fruit' then
                weaponSc('Blox Fruit')

                if p46 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p46 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                elseif p46 == 'C' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'C', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'C', false, game)
                elseif p46 == 'V' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'V', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'V', false, game)
                end
            elseif p45 == 'Gun' then
                weaponSc('Gun')

                if p46 == 'Z' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Z', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Z', false, game)
                elseif p46 == 'X' then
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'X', false, game)
                    vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'X', false, game)
                end
            end
            if p45 == 'nil' and p46 == 'Y' then
                vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, 'Y', false, game)
                vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, 'Y', false, game)
            end
        end

        local v47 = getrawmetatable(game)
        local vu48 = v47.__namecall

        setreadonly(v47, false)

        v47.__namecall = newcclosure(function(...)
            local v49 = getnamecallmethod()
            local v50 = {...}

            if tostring(v49) ~= 'FireServer' or (tostring(v50[1]) ~= 'RemoteEvent' or (tostring(v50[2]) == 'true' or tostring(v50[2]) == 'false')) or (not _G.FarmMastery_G or SoulGuitar) and (not _G.FarmMastery_Dev and (not _G.FarmBlazeEM and (not _G.Prehis_Skills and (not _G.SeaBeast1 and (not _G.FishBoat and (not _G.PGB and (not _G.Leviathan1 and (not _G.Complete_Trials and (not _G.AimMethod or ABmethod ~= 'AimBots Skill')))))))) and (not _G.AimMethod or ABmethod ~= 'Auto Aimbots')) then
                return vu48(...)
            end

            v50[2] = MousePos

            return vu48(unpack(v50))
        end)

        function GetConnectionEnemies(p51)
            local v52, v53, v54 = pairs(replicated:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v55

                v54, v55 = v52(v53, v54)

                if v54 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v55:IsA('Model') and (typeof(p51) == 'table' and table.find(p51, v55.Name) or v55.Name == p51) and (v55:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and v55.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
                    return v55
                end
            end

            local v56 = next
            local v57, v58 = game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()

            while true do
                local v59

                v58, v59 = v56(v57, v58)

                if v58 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v59:IsA('Model') and (typeof(p51) == 'table' and table.find(p51, v59.Name) or v59.Name == p51) and (v59:FindFirstChild('Humanoid') and v59.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
                    return v59
                end
            end
        end
        function LowCpu()
            local v60 = game
            local v61 = v60.Workspace
            local v62 = v60.Lighting
            local v63 = v61.Terrain

            v63.WaterWaveSize = 0
            v63.WaterWaveSpeed = 0
            v63.WaterReflectance = 0
            v63.WaterTransparency = 0
            v62.GlobalShadows = false
            v62.FogEnd = 9000000000
            v62.Brightness = 0
            settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = 'Level01'

            local v64, v65, v66 = pairs(v60:GetDescendants())
            local v67 = true

            while true do
                local v68

                v66, v68 = v64(v65, v66)

                if v66 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v68:IsA('Part') or (v68:IsA('Union') or (v68:IsA('CornerWedgePart') or v68:IsA('TrussPart'))) then
                    v68.Material = 'Plastic'
                    v68.Reflectance = 0
                elseif v68:IsA('Decal') or v68:IsA('Texture') and v67 then
                    v68.Transparency = 1
                elseif v68:IsA('ParticleEmitter') or v68:IsA('Trail') then
                    v68.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0)
                elseif v68:IsA('Explosion') then
                    v68.BlastPressure = 1
                    v68.BlastRadius = 1
                elseif v68:IsA('Fire') or (v68:IsA('SpotLight') or (v68:IsA('Smoke') or v68:IsA('Sparkles'))) then
                    v68.Enabled = false
                elseif v68:IsA('MeshPart') then
                    v68.Material = 'Plastic'
                    v68.Reflectance = 0
                    v68.TextureID = 1.0385902758728955e16
                end
            end

            local v69, v70, v71 = pairs(v62:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v72

                v71, v72 = v69(v70, v71)

                if v71 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v72:IsA('BlurEffect') or (v72:IsA('SunRaysEffect') or (v72:IsA('ColorCorrectionEffect') or (v72:IsA('BloomEffect') or v72:IsA('DepthOfFieldEffect')))) then
                    v72.Enabled = false
                end
            end
        end
        function CheckF()
            if GetBP('Dragon-Dragon') or (GetBP('Gas-Gas') or (GetBP('Yeti-Yeti') or (GetBP('Kitsune-Kitsune') or GetBP('T-Rex-T-Rex')))) then
                return true
            end
        end
        function CheckBoat()
            local v73, v74, v75 = pairs(workspace.Boats:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v76

                v75, v76 = v73(v74, v75)

                if v75 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if tostring(v76.Owner.Value) == tostring(plr.Name) then
                    return v76
                end
            end

            return false
        end

                    break

                    return true
                end
            end

            return false
        end

        function DropFruits()
            local v115 = next
            local v116, v117 = plr.Backpack:GetChildren()

            while true do
                local v118

                v117, v118 = v115(v116, v117)

                if v117 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if string.find(v118.Name, 'Fruit') then
                    EquipWeapon(v118.Name)
                    wait(0.1)

                    if plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible == true then
                        plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible = false
                    end

                    EquipWeapon(v118.Name)
                    plr.Character:FindFirstChild(v118.Name).EatRemote:InvokeServer('Drop')
                end
            end

            local v119, v120, v121 = pairs(plr.Character:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v122

                v121, v122 = v119(v120, v121)

                if v121 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if string.find(v122.Name, 'Fruit') then
                    EquipWeapon(v122.Name)
                    wait(0.1)

                    if plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible == true then
                        plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible = false
                    end

                    EquipWeapon(v122.Name)
                    plr.Character:FindFirstChild(v122.Name).EatRemote:InvokeServer('Drop')
                end
            end
        end

        function GetIn(p124)
            local v125, v126, v127 = pairs(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('getInventory'))

            while true do
                local v128

                v127, v128 = v125(v126, v127)

                if v127 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if type(v128) == 'table' and (v128.Name == p124 or (plr.Character:FindFirstChild(p124) or plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(p124))) then
                    return true
                end
            end

            return false
        end
        function GetM(p129)
            local v130, v131, v132 = pairs(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('getInventory'))

            while true do
                local v133

                v132, v133 = v130(v131, v132)

                if v132 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if type(v133) == 'table' and (v133.Type == 'Material' and v133.Name == p129) then
                    return v133.Count
                end
            end

            return 0
        end

        function getInfinity_Ability(p139, pu140)
            if Root then
                if p139 == 'Soru' and pu140 then
                    local v141 = next
                    local v142, v143 = getgc()

                    while true do
                        local v144

                        v143, v144 = v141(v142, v143)

                        if v143 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if plr.Character.Soru and (typeof(v144) == 'function' and getfenv(v144).script == plr.Character.Soru) then
                            local v145 = next
                            local v146, v147 = getupvalues(v144)

                            while true do
                                local v148

                                v147, v148 = v145(v146, v147)

                                if v147 == nil then
                                    break
                                end
                                if typeof(v148) == 'table' then
                                    repeat
                                        wait(Sec)

                                        v148.LastUse = 0
                                    until not pu140 or plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                elseif p139 == 'Energy' and pu140 then
                    plr.Character.Energy.Changed:connect(function()
                        if pu140 then
                            plr.Character.Energy.Value = Energy
                        end
                    end)
                elseif p139 == 'Observation' and pu140 then
                    plr.VisionRadius.Value = math.huge
                end
            end
        end
        function Hop()
            pcall(function()
                for v149 = math.random(1, math.random(40, 75)), 100 do
                    local v150 = replicated.__ServerBrowser:InvokeServer(v149)
                    local v151 = next
                    local v152 = nil

                    while true do
                        local v153

                        v152, v153 = v151(v150, v152)

                        if v152 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if tonumber(v153.Count) < 12 then
                            TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, v152)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        end

        function _tp(p168)
            local v169 = plr.Character

            if v169 and v169:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') then
                local v170 = v169.HumanoidRootPart
                local v171 = (p168.Position - v170.Position).Magnitude
                local v172 = TweenInfo.new(v171 / 300, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                local vu173 = game:GetService('TweenService'):Create(vu154, v172, {CFrame = p168})

                if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true then
                    vu154.CFrame = CFrame.new(vu154.Position.X, p168.Y, vu154.Position.Z)
                end

                vu173:Play()
                task.spawn(function()
                    while vu173.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
                        if not shouldTween then
                            vu173:Cancel()

                            break
                        end

                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
        function TeleportToTarget(p174)
            if (p174.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 1000 then
                _tp(p174)
            else
                _tp(p174)
            end
        end

        function BTP(p176)
            local v177 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local v178 = v177.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            local v179 = v177.Character.Humanoid
            local v180 = v177.PlayerGui.Main
            local _ = p176.Position
            local v181 = v178.Position

            while true do
                v179.Health = 0
                v178.CFrame = p176
                v180.Quest.Visible = false

                if (v178.Position - v181).Magnitude > 1 then
                    v181 = v178.Position
                    v178.CFrame = p176
                end

                task.wait(0.5)

                if (p176.Position - v178.Position).Magnitude <= 2000 then
                    return
                end
            end
        end

        function QuestBeta()
            QuestB()

            return {
                [0] = _G.FindBoss,
                [1] = bMon,
                [2] = Qdata,
                [3] = Qname,
                [4] = PosB,
                [5] = PosQBoss,
            }
        end

        function MaterialMon()
            local v189 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local vu190 = v189.Character

            if vu190 then
                vu190 = v189.Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')
            end
            if vu190 then
                function shouldRequestEntrance(p191, p192)
                    if p192 <= (vu190.Position - p191).Magnitude then
                        replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer('requestEntrance', p191)
                    end
                end

                if World1 then
                    if SelectMaterial ~= 'Angel Wings' then
                        if SelectMaterial ~= 'Leather + Scrap Metal' then
                            if SelectMaterial ~= 'Magma Ore' then
                                if SelectMaterial == 'Fish Tail' then

                    end
                elseif World2 then

                ['Hot pink'] = 'Winter Sky',

                return v532[tostring(p531.BrickColor)]
            end
        end

            function getT(p794)
                local v795 = nil

                if p794 == 1 then
                    v795 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment1.Line.Rotation
                elseif p794 == 3 then
                    v795 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment3.Line.Rotation
                elseif p794 == 4 then
                    v795 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment4.Line.Rotation
                elseif p794 == 7 then
                    v795 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment7.Line.Rotation
                elseif p794 == 10 then
                    v795 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Tablet.Segment10.Line.Rotation
                end
                if v795 then
                    return v795.Z
                end
            end
            function getRT(p796)
                local v797 = workspace.Map['Haunted Castle'].Trophies.Quest
                local v798, v799, v800 = pairs(v797:GetChildren())
                local v801 = nil

                while true do
                    local v802

                    v800, v802 = v798(v799, v800)

                    if v800 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if p796 == 1 and (v802.Name == 'Trophy1' and v802:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                        v801 = v802.Handle.Rotation
                    elseif p796 == 2 and (v802.Name == 'Trophy2' and v802:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                        v801 = v802.Handle.Rotation
                    elseif p796 == 3 and (v802.Name == 'Trophy3' and v802:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                        v801 = v802.Handle.Rotation
                    elseif p796 == 4 and (v802.Name == 'Trophy4' and v802:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                        v801 = v802.Handle.Rotation
                    elseif p796 == 5 and (v802.Name == 'Trophy5' and v802:FindFirstChild('Handle')) then
                        v801 = v802.Handle.Rotation
                    end
                    if v801 then
                        return v801.Z
                    end
                end
            end

            function GetSeaBeastTrial()
                if not workspace.Map:FindFirstChild('FishmanTrial') then
                    return nil
                end
                if workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Trial of Water') then
                    FishmanTrial = workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild('Trial of Water')
                end
                if FishmanTrial then
                    local v832 = next
                    local v833, v834 = workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren()

                    while true do
                        local v835

                        v834, v835 = v832(v833, v834)

                        if v834 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v835:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and ((v835.HumanoidRootPart.Position - FishmanTrial.Position).Magnitude <= 1500 and v835.Health.Value > 0) then
                            return v835
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            spawn(function()
                while wait(Sec) do
                    pcall(function()
                        if _G.Complete_Trials and tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == 'Mink' then
                            notween(workspace.Map.MinkTrial.Ceiling.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -20, 0))
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end)
            spawn(function()
                while wait(Sec) do
                    pcall(function()
                        if _G.Complete_Trials and (tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == 'Fishman' and GetSeaBeastTrial()) then

                                MousePos = GetSeaBeastTrial().HumanoidRootPart.Position

            function checkQuesta()
                local vu848 = {
                    {
                        Context = 'Check',
                    },
                }
                local vu849 = nil

                pcall(function()
                    local v850 = {
                        {
                            Context = 'RequestQuest',
                        },
                    }

                    game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):WaitForChild('Modules'):WaitForChild('Net'):WaitForChild('RF/DragonHunter'):InvokeServer(unpack(v850))
                end)

                local _, _ = pcall(function()
                    vu849 = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):WaitForChild('Modules'):WaitForChild('Net'):WaitForChild('RF/DragonHunter'):InvokeServer(unpack(vu848))
                end)
                local v851 = nil
                local v852 = nil
                local v853 = nil
                local v854, v855

                if vu849 and vu849.Text then
                    v854 = true

                    local v856 = vu849.Text

                    if string.find(tostring(v856), 'Defeat') then
                        local v857 = string.sub(tostring(v856), 8, 9)

                        v851 = tonumber(v857)

                        local v858, v859, v860 = pairs({
                            'Hydra Enforcer',
                            'Venomous Assailant',
                        })

                        v853 = 1

                        while true do
                            v860, v855 = v858(v859, v860)

                            if v860 == nil then
                                v855 = v852

                                break
                            end
                            if string.find(v856, v855) then
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    elseif string.find(tostring(v856), 'Destroy') then
                        v855 = nil
                        v851 = 10
                        v853 = 2
                    else
                        v855 = v852
                    end
                else
                    v855 = v852
                    v854 = false
                end

                return v854, v855, v851, v853
            end
            function BackTODoJo()
                local v861, v862, v863 = pairs(game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Notifications:GetChildren())

                while true do
                    local v864

                    v863, v864 = v861(v862, v863)

                    if v863 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if v864.Name == 'NotificationTemplate' and string.find(v864.Text, 'Head back to the Dojo to complete more tasks') then
                        return true
                    end
                end

                return false
            end
            function DragonMobClear(p865, p866, p867)
                if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild(p866) then
                    local v868, v869, v870 = pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

                    while true do
                        local v871

                        v870, v871 = v868(v869, v870)

                        if v870 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v871.Name == p866 and (vu19.Alive(v871) and p865) then
                            vu19.Kill(v871, p865)
                        end
                    end
                else
                    _tp(p867)
                end
            end

        local function vu1111(p1110)

        function EspPly()
            local v1112 = next
            local v1113, v1114 = game.Players:GetChildren()

            while true do
                local vu1115

                v1114, vu1115 = v1112(v1113, v1114)

                if v1114 == nil then
                    break
                end

                pcall(function()
                    if not isnil(vu1115.Character) then
                        if PlayerEsp then
                            if isnil(vu1115.Character.Head) or vu1115.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number) then
                                vu1115.Character.Head['NameEsp' .. Number].TextLabel.Text = vu1115.Data.Level.Value .. ' | ' .. vu1115.Name .. ' | ' .. vu1111((game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - vu1115.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. ' M\nHealth : ' .. vu1111(vu1115.Character.Humanoid.Health * 100 / vu1115.Character.Humanoid.MaxHealth) .. '%'
                            else
                                local v1116 = Instance.new('BillboardGui', vu1115.Character.Head)

                                v1116.Name = 'NameEsp' .. Number
                                v1116.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
                                v1116.Size = UDim2.new(1, 200, 1, 30)
                                v1116.Adornee = vu1115.Character.Head
                                v1116.AlwaysOnTop = true

                                local v1117 = Instance.new('TextLabel', v1116)

                                v1117.Font = Enum.Font.Code
                                v1117.FontSize = 'Size14'
                                v1117.TextWrapped = true
                                v1117.Text = vu1115.Name .. ' \n' .. vu1111((game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - vu1115.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. ' M'
                                v1117.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                                v1117.TextYAlignment = 'Top'
                                v1117.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                                v1117.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5

                                if vu1115.Team ~= TeamSelf then
                                    v1117.TextColor3 = Color3.new(255, 0, 0)
                                else
                                    v1117.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 254)
                                end
                            end
                        elseif vu1115.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number) then
                            vu1115.Character.Head:FindFirstChild('NameEsp' .. Number):Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        function ChestEsp()
            if ChestESP then
                local v1166 = game:GetService('CollectionService')
                local v1167 = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
                local v1168 = (v1167.Character or v1167.CharacterAdded:Wait()):GetPivot().Position
                local v1169 = v1166:GetTagged('_ChestTagged')
                local v1170, v1171, v1172 = ipairs(v1169)

                while true do
                    local vu1173

                    v1172, vu1173 = v1170(v1171, v1172)

                    if v1172 == nil then
                        break
                    end

                    local v1174

                    if SelectedIsland and not vu1173:IsDescendantOf(SelectedIsland) or vu1173:GetAttribute('IsDisabled') then
                        v1174 = true
                    end

                    local v1175, v1176 = pcall(function()
                        return vu1173:GetPivot().Position
                    end)

                    if not v1175 then
                        if not vu1173:IsA('BasePart') then
                            v1174 = true
                        end

                        v1176 = vu1173.Position
                    end

                    local v1177 = (v1176 - v1168).Magnitude

                    vu1173:GetFullName():gsub('[^%w_]', '_')

                    local v1178 = vu1173:FindFirstChild('ChestEspAttachment')

                    if not v1178 then
                        local v1179 = Instance.new('Attachment')

                        v1179.Name = 'ChestEspAttachment'
                        v1179.Parent = vu1173
                        v1179.Position = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)

                        local v1180 = Instance.new('BillboardGui')

                        v1180.Name = 'NameEsp'
                        v1180.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 30)
                        v1180.Adornee = v1179
                        v1180.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
                        v1180.AlwaysOnTop = true
                        v1180.Parent = v1179

                        local v1181 = Instance.new('TextLabel')

                        v1181.Font = Enum.Font.Code
                        v1181.TextSize = 14
                        v1181.TextWrapped = true
                        v1181.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                        v1181.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top
                        v1181.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                        v1181.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
                        v1181.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 245, 245)
                        v1181.Parent = v1180
                    end

                    local v1182

                    if v1178 then
                        v1182 = v1178:FindFirstChild('NameEsp')
                    else
                        v1182 = v1178
                    end
                    if v1182 then
                        local v1183 = math.floor(v1177 / 3)
                        local v1184 = vu1173.Name:gsub('Label', '')

                        v1182.TextLabel.Text = string.format('[%s] %d M', v1184, v1183)
                    end
                    if _G_AutoFarmChest and (v1177 <= 20 and v1178) then
                        v1178:Destroy()

                        v1174 = true
                    else
                        v1174 = true
                    end
                    if not v1174 then
                        break
                    end
                end
            else
                local v1185, v1186, v1187 = ipairs(game:GetService('CollectionService'):GetTagged('_ChestTagged'))

                while true do
                    local v1188

                    v1187, v1188 = v1185(v1186, v1187)

                    if v1187 == nil then
                        break
                    end

                    local v1189 = v1188:FindFirstChild('ChestEspAttachment')

                    if v1189 then
                        v1189:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        function berriesEsp()
            if BerryEsp then
                local v1190 = game:GetService('CollectionService')
                local v1191 = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
                local v1192 = v1190:GetTagged('BerryBush')
                local v1193, v1194, v1195 = ipairs(v1192)

                while true do

                    v1195, v1196 = v1193(v1194, v1195)

                    if v1195 == nil then

                    local v1197 = v1196.Parent:GetPivot().Position

                    while true do
                        local v1201

                        v1200, v1201 = v1198(v1199, v1200)

                        if v1200 == nil then
                            break
                        end

                                v1203.CanCollide = false
                                v1203.Parent = workspace
                                v1203.CFrame = CFrame.new(v1197)

                    local function vu1252(p1248, p1249)
                        local v1250 = bit32.band(p1248, 65535) + bit32.band(p1249, 65535)
                        local v1251 = bit32.rshift(p1248, 16) + bit32.rshift(p1249, 16) + bit32.rshift(v1250, 16)

                        return bit32.bor(bit32.lshift(v1251, 16), bit32.band(v1250, 65535))
                    end
                    local function vu1255(p1253, p1254)
                        return bit32.bor(bit32.lshift(p1253, p1254), bit32.rshift(p1253, 32 - p1254))
                    end
                    local function vu1259(p1256, p1257, p1258)
                        return bit32.bor(bit32.band(p1256, p1257), bit32.band(bit32.bnot(p1256), p1258))
                    end
                    local function vu1263(p1260, p1261, p1262)
                        return bit32.bor(bit32.band(p1260, p1262), bit32.band(p1261, bit32.bnot(p1262)))
                    end
                    local function vu1267(p1264, p1265, p1266)
                        return bit32.bxor(p1264, bit32.bxor(p1265, p1266))
                    end
                    local function vu1271(p1268, p1269, p1270)
                        return bit32.bxor(p1269, bit32.bor(p1268, bit32.bnot(p1270)))
                    end

                    function vu1244.sum(p1272)
                        local v1273 = #p1272
                        local v1274 = p1272 .. '\u{fffd}'
                        local v1275 = 1732584193
                        local v1276 = 4023233417
                        local v1277 = 2562383102
                        local v1278 = 271733878

                        while#v1274 % 64 ~= 56 do
                            v1274 = v1274 .. '\0'
                        end

                        local v1279 = v1273 * 8
                        local v1280 = ''

                        for v1281 = 0, 7 do
                            v1280 = v1280 .. string.char(bit32.band(bit32.rshift(v1279, v1281 * 8), 255))
                        end

                        local v1282 = v1274 .. v1280

                        for v1283 = 1, #v1282, 64 do
                            local v1284 = v1282:sub(v1283, v1283 + 63)
                            local v1285 = {}

                            for v1286 = 0, 15 do
                                local v1287, v1288, v1289, v1290 = v1284:byte(v1286 * 4 + 1, v1286 * 4 + 4)

                                v1285[v1286] = bit32.bor(v1287, bit32.lshift(v1288, 8), bit32.lshift(v1289, 16), bit32.lshift(v1290, 24))
                            end

                            local v1292 = v1276
                            local v1293 = v1275
                            local v1294 = v1278
                            local v1295 = {
                                7,
                                12,
                                17,
                                22,
                                5,
                                9,
                                14,
                                20,
                                4,
                                11,
                                16,
                                23,
                                6,
                                10,
                                15,
                                21,
                            }

                            for v1296 = 0, 63 do
                                local v1297, v1298, v1299

                                if v1296 < 16 then
                                    v1297 = vu1259(v1276, v1277, v1278)
                                    v1298 = v1296 % 4
                                    v1299 = v1296
                                elseif v1296 < 32 then
                                    v1297 = vu1263(v1276, v1277, v1278)
                                    v1299 = (1 + 5 * v1296) % 16
                                    v1298 = 4 + v1296 % 4
                                elseif v1296 < 48 then
                                    v1297 = vu1267(v1276, v1277, v1278)
                                    v1299 = (5 + 3 * v1296) % 16

                                else
                                    v1297 = vu1271(v1276, v1277, v1278)
                                    v1299 = 7 * v1296 % 16
                                    v1298 = 12 + v1296 % 4
                                end

                                v1275 = v1278
                                v1278 = v1277
                                v1277 = v1276
                                v1276 = v1300
                            end

                            v1275 = vu1252(v1275, v1293)
                            v1276 = vu1252(v1276, v1292)
                            v1277 = vu1252(v1277, v1291)
                            v1278 = vu1252(v1278, v1294)
                        end

                        local function v1304(p1301)
                            local v1302 = ''

                            for v1303 = 0, 3 do
                                v1302 = v1302 .. string.char(bit32.band(bit32.rshift(p1301, v1303 * 8), 255))
                            end

                            return v1302
                        end

                        return v1304(v1275) .. v1304(v1276) .. v1304(v1277) .. v1304(v1278)
                    end
                    function vu1245.new(p1305, p1306, p1307)
                        if #p1305 > 64 then
                            p1305 = p1307(p1305)
                        end

                        local v1308 = ''
                        local v1309 = ''

                        for v1310 = 1, 64 do
                            local v1311 = v1310 > #p1305 and 0 or (string.byte(p1305, v1310) or 0)

                            v1308 = v1308 .. string.char(bit32.bxor(v1311, 92))
                            v1309 = v1309 .. string.char(bit32.bxor(v1311, 54))
                        end

                        return p1307(v1308 .. p1307(v1309 .. p1306))
                    end

                    local vu1312 = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/'

                    function vu1246.encode(p1313)
                        return (p1313:gsub('.', function(p1314)
                            local v1315 = p1314:byte()
                            local v1316 = ''

                            for v1317 = 8, 1, -1 do
                                v1316 = v1316 .. (v1315 % 2 ^ v1317 - v1315 % 2 ^ (v1317 - 1) > 0 and '1' or '0')
                            end

                            return v1316
                        end) .. '0000'):gsub('%d%d%d?%d?%d?%d?', function(p1318)
                            if #p1318 < 6 then
                                return ''
                            end

                            local v1319 = 0

                            for v1320 = 1, 6 do
                                v1319 = v1319 + (p1318:sub(v1320, v1320) == '1' and 2 ^ (6 - v1320) or 0)
                            end

                            return vu1312:sub(v1319 + 1, v1319 + 1)
                        end) .. ({
                            '',
                            '==',
                            '=',
                        })[#p1313 % 3 + 1]
                    end

                    local function v1334(p1321)

        function AttackNoCoolDown()
            local v1415 = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
            local v1416 = v1415.Character

            if not v1416 then
                return
            end

            local v1417, v1418, v1419 = ipairs(v1416:GetChildren())
            local v1420 = nil

            while true do
                local v1421

                v1419, v1421 = v1417(v1418, v1419)

                if v1419 == nil then
                    v1421 = v1420

                    break
                end
                if v1421:IsA('Tool') then
                    break
                end
            end

            if v1421 then
                local v1422 = vu1414(v1416, 60)

                if #v1422 ~= 0 then
                    local v1423 = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage')
                    local vu1424 = v1423:FindFirstChild('Modules')

                    if vu1424 then

                        if v1425 and v1426 then
                            local v1427, v1428, v1429 = ipairs(v1422)
                            local v1430 = {}
                            local v1431 = nil

                            while true do
                                local v1432

                                v1429, v1432 = v1427(v1428, v1429)

                                if v1429 == nil then
                                    break
                                end
                                if not v1432:GetAttribute('IsBoat') then
                                    local v1433 = {
                                        'RightLowerArm',
                                        'RightUpperArm',
                                        'LeftLowerArm',
                                        'LeftUpperArm',
                                        'RightHand',
                                        'LeftHand',
                                    }
                                    local v1434 = v1432:FindFirstChild(v1433[math.random(#v1433)]) or v1432.PrimaryPart

                                    if v1434 then
                                        table.insert(v1430, {v1432, v1434})

                                        v1431 = v1434
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            if v1431 then
                                v1425:FireServer(0)

                                local v1435 = v1415:FindFirstChild('PlayerScripts')

                                if v1435 then
                                    local v1436 = v1435:FindFirstChildOfClass('LocalScript')

                                    while not v1436 do
                                        v1435.ChildAdded:Wait()

                                        v1436 = v1435:FindFirstChildOfClass('LocalScript')
                                    end

                                    local v1437 = nil

                                    if getsenv then
                                        local v1438, v1439 = pcall(getsenv, v1436)

                                        if v1438 and v1439 then
                                            v1437 = v1439._G.SendHitsToServer
                                        end
                                    end

                                    local v1440, v1441 = pcall(function()
                                        return require(vu1424.Flags).COMBAT_REMOTE_THREAD or false
                                    end)

                                    if v1440 and (v1441 and v1437) then
                                        v1437(v1431, v1430)
                                    elseif v1440 and not v1441 then
                                        v1426:FireServer(v1431, v1430)
                                    end
                                end
                            else
                                return
                            end
                        else
                            return
                        end
                    else
                        return
                    end
                else
                    return
                end
            else
                return
            end
        end

        function get_Monster()
            local v1442, v1443, v1444 = pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v1445

                v1444, v1445 = v1442(v1443, v1444)

                if v1444 == nil then
                    break
                end

                local v1446 = v1445:FindFirstChild('UpperTorso') or v1445:FindFirstChild('Head')

                if v1445:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart', true) and (v1446 and (v1445.Head.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 50) then
                    return true, v1446.Position
                end
            end

            local v1447, v1448, v1449 = pairs(workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v1450

                v1449, v1450 = v1447(v1448, v1449)

                if v1449 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v1450:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') and (v1450:FindFirstChild('Health') and v1450.Health.Value > 0) then
                    return true, v1450.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                end
            end

            local v1451, v1452, v1453 = pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren())

            while true do
                local v1454

                v1453, v1454 = v1451(v1452, v1453)

                if v1453 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if v1454:FindFirstChild('Health') and (v1454.Health.Value > 0 and v1454:FindFirstChild('VehicleSeat')) then
                    return true, v1454.Engine.Position
                end
            end
        end
        function Actived()
            local v1455 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool')
            local v1456 = next
            local v1457, v1458 = getconnections(v1455.Activated)

            while true do
                local v1459

                v1458, v1459 = v1456(v1457, v1458)

                if v1458 == nil then
                    break
                end
                if typeof(v1459.Function) == 'function' then
                    getupvalues(v1459.Function)
                end
            end
        end
